Function: services._fun_service_point(service_request json)

Returns: json

Language: PLV8

var R = {response: []};

if(service_request.requests && service_request.header){

	service_request.requests.forEach(function(req){

		plv8.elog(NOTICE, "req = ", JSON.stringify(req));

		if(req.service && req.service.length > 0){

			R.error = 0;
			plv8.elog(NOTICE, "req = ", 1);

			try{

				var token = service_request.header.token||'';
				var fun_service = plv8.find_function('services.funjs_'+req.service);
				var service = plv8.execute( 'SELECT services.fun_check_service($1::TEXT, $2::TEXT);', [ req.service, token ] )[0].fun_check_service;

				var r = {service: req.service, response: []};

				switch(service.error){
					case 0:
					r.response = fun_service(service_request.header, req);
					R.response.push(r);
					break;
					default:
					r.message = service.message;
					r.error = service.error+4;
					R.response.push(r);
					break;
				}

			}catch(e){
				R.message = e.message;
				R.error = 2;
			}


		}else{
			R.message = 'Did not specify the service';
			R.error = 1;
		}

	});
	
}else{
	R.message = 'Did not specify the request o header';
	R.error = 3;
}


return R;

Function: services._funjs_login_user(user_credentials json)

Returns: json

Language: PLV8

var R = {iduser: 0, token: '', error: 0, message: ''};

if(user_credentials && user_credentials.user && user_credentials.pwd && user_credentials.ip && user_credentials.user_agent){

/*
//SELECT iduser, username, ts, footprint_row, idcontact, enabled, user_start, 
       user_end, pwd, user_role, divisions, accounts, locked_date, failed_access_attempts, 
       email_notification, xmpp_notification, admin_attention_group
  FROM users.users;
*/

var user = plv8.execute( 'SELECT * FROM users.users WHERE username = $1 AND pwd = md5($2) LIMIT 1;', [user_credentials.user, user_credentials.pwd]);

//plv8.elog(NOTICE, "U = ", JSON.stringify(user));

if(user.length > 0){

R.iduser = user[0].iduser;
plv8.execute( 'DELETE FROM users.tokens WHERE isuser = true AND id = $1;', [R.iduser]);
var token = plv8.execute( 'INSERT INTO users.tokens(token, isuser, id, first_heartbeat, last_heartbeat) VALUES ($1, true, $2, now(), now()) RETURNING token;', [plv8.find_function("funjs_md5")(JSON.stringify(user)+Date.now()), R.iduser]);
if(token.length > 0){
R.token = token[0].token;
}

//plv8.elog(NOTICE, "t = ", JSON.stringify(token));

}else{
R.error = 2;
R.message = 'Usuario o clave invalida';
}

}else{
R.error = 1;
R.message = 'Las credenciales no estan completas';
plv8.elog(NOTICE, "Error = ", 'Sin credeneciles No valido');
}

return R;

Function: services.create_uuid_reg()

Returns: trigger

Language: PLPGSQL

BEGIN

NEW.idreg := md5(NEW.data::TEXT)::UUID;

RETURN NEW;
END;

Function: services.fun_check_service(itoken text, service text)

Returns: json

Language: PLPGSQL

DECLARE
R json;
ispublic boolean default false;
id BIGINT DEFAULT -100;

BEGIN

SELECT idservice, is_public INTO id, ispublic FROM services.services WHERE service_name = service AND enabled = true;

IF id < 1 OR id IS NULL THEN

--IF EXISTS(SELECT * FROM information_schema.routines WHERE  specific_schema LIKE 'services' AND routine_name LIKE 'funjs_'||service) AND NOT EXISTS(SELECT * FROM services.services WHERE service_name = service) THEN
--INSERT INTO services.services (service_name) VALUES (service);
--END IF;

R := json_build_object('idservice',-1,'error',1, 'message', 'El servicio no existe o no esta habilitado');

ELSE

R := json_build_object('idservice',id,'error',0, 'message', '');

IF ispublic = FALSE AND NOT EXISTS(SELECT * FROM users.tokens WHERE users.tokens.token::TEXT = itoken) THEN
	R := json_build_object('idservice',-2,'error',2, 'message', 'Es requerido un token valido para este servicio');
END IF;


END IF;

RETURN R;
END;

Function: services.fun_eta_interface_txt(message text, delivery_status json)

Returns: SET OF record

Language: PLPGSQL

DECLARE
R TEXT[];
e JSON;
ideq BIGINT;
--id BIGINT;
interface TEXT;
iiddivision BIGINT;
iidaccount BIGINT;

BEGIN

-- Valida que exista el id del equipo
--SELECT idequipment INTO ideq FROM equipments WHERE report_validator = devicekey;
SELECT idequipment, iddivision, idaccount INTO ideq, iiddivision, iidaccount FROM view_account_network_devices WHERE report_validator = devicekey;


IF ideq > 0 THEN

FOR e IN SELECT * FROM json_array_elements(list) LOOP 

interface := (e->>'Interface')::TEXT;
idqueue := (e->>'idQueue')::TEXT;
delivery_status := -1;
message := '';

RAISE NOTICE 'NombreArchivo(%)', (e->>'NombreArchivo')::TEXT;
RAISE NOTICE 'FechaCreacionArchivo(%)', (e->>'FechaCreacionArchivo')::TEXT;
RAISE NOTICE 'NombreArchivo(%)', (e->>'NombreArchivo')::TEXT;
RAISE NOTICE 'NumLinea(%)', (e->>'NumLinea')::TEXT;
RAISE NOTICE 'Interface(%)', interface;
RAISE NOTICE 'DatosLinea(%)', (e->>'DatosLinea')::TEXT;

IF interface IS NOT NULL THEN

BEGIN 
INSERT INTO secondary.interfaces_eta_rm_matriz(
            namefile, datetimefile, 
            fileline, nameinterface, 
            datas, enmatriz, isvalid, idaccount)
VALUES ((e->>'NombreArchivo')::TEXT, 
(e->>'FechaCreacionArchivo')::TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE, 
            (e->>'NumLinea')::INTEGER, interface, 
            (e->>'DatosLinea')::JSONB, (e->>'EnMatriz')::BOOLEAN, (e->>'EsValido')::BOOLEAN, iidaccount);

            idreg:= currval('secondary.eta_materiales_idregmat_seq'::regclass);
            delivery_status := 0;
            
RAISE NOTICE 'idreg(%)', idreg::text;
RETURN NEXT;

        EXCEPTION WHEN unique_violation THEN
         delivery_status := 1;
message := 'unique_violation';
            -- Do nothing, and loop to try the UPDATE again.
            --R := array_append(R, (e->>'idQueue')::TEXT);
END;

ELSE
delivery_status := 2;
message := 'No contiene interface';


              END IF;
     

      

END LOOP;

END IF;


-- RETURN NEXT;

--RETURN R;
END

Function: services.fun_eta_resultado_validacion_txt_interfaces(message text, delivery_status json)

Returns: SET OF record

Language: PLPGSQL

DECLARE
R TEXT[];
e JSON;
ideq BIGINT;
--id BIGINT;
PrefijoArchivo TEXT;
ipriority INTEGER DEFAULT 10;
iideventtype BIGINT DEFAULT  0;
iiddivision BIGINT DEFAULT  -1;

BEGIN

-- Valida que exista el id del equipo
SELECT idequipment, iddivision INTO ideq, iiddivision FROM view_account_network_devices WHERE report_validator = devicekey;

--SELECT idequipment INTO ideq FROM equipments WHERE report_validator = devicekey;

IF ideq > 0 THEN

FOR e IN SELECT * FROM json_array_elements(list) LOOP 


PrefijoArchivo := (e->>'PrefijoArchivo')::TEXT;
idqueue := (e->>'idQueue')::TEXT;

delivery_status := -1;
message := '';
/*
RAISE NOTICE 'NombreArchivo(%)', (e->>'NombreArchivo')::TEXT;
RAISE NOTICE 'FechaCreacionArchivo(%)', (e->>'FechaCreacionArchivo')::TEXT;
RAISE NOTICE 'NombreArchivo(%)', (e->>'NombreArchivo')::TEXT;
RAISE NOTICE 'NumLinea(%)', (e->>'NumLinea')::TEXT;
RAISE NOTICE 'Interface(%)', interface;
RAISE NOTICE 'DatosLinea(%)', (e->>'DatosLinea')::TEXT;
*/

IF PrefijoArchivo IS NOT NULL THEN

BEGIN 

CASE

WHEN PrefijoArchivo = 'empleados' THEN
iideventtype := 83;
WHEN PrefijoArchivo = 'proveedores' THEN
iideventtype := 88;
WHEN PrefijoArchivo = 'fmapago' THEN
iideventtype := 82;
WHEN PrefijoArchivo = 'tipotxs' THEN
iideventtype := 89;
WHEN PrefijoArchivo = 'fechapago' THEN
iideventtype := 95;
WHEN PrefijoArchivo = 'clientes' THEN
iideventtype := 103;
WHEN PrefijoArchivo = 'direcciones' THEN
iideventtype := 126;
WHEN PrefijoArchivo = 'saldocli' THEN
iideventtype := 133;
WHEN PrefijoArchivo = 'articulos' THEN
iideventtype := 63;
WHEN PrefijoArchivo = 'articulosauxiliar' THEN
iideventtype := 137;
WHEN PrefijoArchivo = 'ventasxmateriales' THEN
iideventtype := 68;


ELSE
iideventtype := 0;
END CASE;

IF (e->>'Resultado')::TEXT = 'false' THEN
ipriority:= 1;
ELSE
ipriority:= 10;
END IF;




INSERT INTO events.datas(
            idaccount, priority, 
            ideventtype, description, details, source)
    VALUES (0, ipriority, 
            iideventtype, (e->>'Mensaje')::TEXT, json_build_object('iddivision',iiddivision)::JSONB, md5(e->>'Archivo'::TEXT)::uuid);
            --iideventtype, (e->>'Mensaje')::TEXT, '{"iddivision": 6}'::jsonb, md5('ETA')::uuid);

/*
INSERT INTO secondary.interfaces_eta_rm_matriz(
            namefile, datetimefile, 
            fileline, nameinterface, 
            datas, enmatriz, isvalid)
VALUES ((e->>'NombreArchivo')::TEXT, 
(e->>'FechaCreacionArchivo')::TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE, 
            (e->>'NumLinea')::INTEGER, interface, 
            (e->>'DatosLinea')::JSONB, (e->>'EnMatriz')::BOOLEAN, (e->>'EsValido')::BOOLEAN);

            idreg:= currval('secondary.eta_materiales_idregmat_seq'::regclass);
            delivery_status := 0;
            */
            
RAISE NOTICE 'idreg(%)', idreg::text;
RETURN NEXT;

        EXCEPTION WHEN unique_violation THEN
         delivery_status := 1;
message := 'unique_violation';
            -- Do nothing, and loop to try the UPDATE again.
            --R := array_append(R, (e->>'idQueue')::TEXT);
END;

ELSE
delivery_status := 2;
message := 'No contiene interface';


              END IF;
     

      

END LOOP;

END IF;


-- RETURN NEXT;

--RETURN R;
END

Function: services.fun_event_receiver(list_events text, devicekey json)

Returns: text[]

Language: PLPGSQL

DECLARE
R TEXT[];
e JSON;
id BIGINT;

BEGIN

SELECT idequipment INTO id FROM equipments WHERE report_validator = devicekey;

FOR e IN SELECT * FROM json_array_elements(list_events) LOOP 


        BEGIN

INSERT INTO events.datas(
            dateevent, ideventtype, description, idequipment, source, details)
VALUES ((e->>'dateevent')::timestamptz, (e->>'ideventtype')::BIGINT, e->>'description'::TEXT, id, (e->>'source')::UUID, (e->>'details_json')::JSONB);

R := array_append(R, (e->>'idQueue')::TEXT);

        EXCEPTION WHEN unique_violation THEN
            -- Do nothing, and loop to try the UPDATE again.
            R := array_append(R, (e->>'idQueue')::TEXT);
        END;



END LOOP;

RETURN R;
END

Function: services.funjs_dbstructure(request json, header json)

Returns: json

Language: PLV8

var R = [];
// Aqui el header es unicamente para obtener informacion que pueda ser necesaria para el request
if(request && header){

	try{

		if(Array.isArray(request)){

			var plan = plv8.prepare( 'SELECT gui.funjs_db_structure($1) as return;', ['TEXT'] );

			request.forEach(function(item) {
				var ritem = {};
				var service = plan.execute([item.datas.tschema_tname] )[0].return;

				ritem.key = item.key;
				ritem.datas = service;
				R.push(ritem);
			});
			
			plan.free();
		}else{
			R.message = 'content not is array';
			R.error = 3;
		}


//R.response.push({idrequest: 'ASSASJBBJ767862J312B', idevent: 0});
//R.response.push({idrequest: '000ASSASJBBJ767862J312B', idevent: 20});

}catch(Error){
	R.message = Error.message;
	R.error = 2;
}

}else{
	R.message = 'No esta definido request o header';
	R.Error = 1;
}



return R;

Function: services.funjs_login_comunicator(credentials json)

var R = {id: 0, token: '', error: 0, message: ''};

if(credentials && credentials.idcommunicator && credentials.pwd && credentials.ip){

/*
SELECT idcommunicator, ts, footprint_row, pwd, enabled, datetime_start, 
       datetime_end, description
  FROM services.communicators;
*/

var communicators = plv8.execute( 'SELECT * FROM services.communicators WHERE idcommunicator = $1 AND pwd = $2;', [credentials.idcommunicator, credentials.pwd]);

//plv8.elog(NOTICE, "U = ", JSON.stringify(communicators));

R.id = communicators[0].idcommunicator;

var token = plv8.execute( 'INSERT INTO users.tokens(token, isuser, id, first_heartbeat, last_heartbeat) VALUES ($1, FALSE, $2, now(), now()) RETURNING token;', [plv8.find_function("funjs_md5")(JSON.stringify(communicators)+Date.now()), R.id]);
if(token.length > 0){
R.token = token[0].token;
}

//plv8.elog(NOTICE, "t = ", JSON.stringify(token));

}else{
R.error = 2;
R.message = 'Usuario o clave invalida';
}

}else{
R.error = 1;
R.message = 'Las credenciales no estan completas';
plv8.elog(NOTICE, "Error = ", 'Sin credeneciles No valido');
}

return R;

Function: services.funjs_point(service_request json)

Returns: json

Language: PLV8

var R = []; // Esta es una matriz porque es posible que se reciba una serie de requerimientos en la misma solicitud
var r = {service: 'service_point'}; // Esta es una respuesta que devolvera esta funcion, en la mayoria de los casos esta variable no deberia usarse y deberia ser parte de la respuesta del servicio final
	if(service_request.body && service_request.cookies){
plv8.elog(NOTICE, "Revisa body y cokoies");
		if(service_request.service && service_request.service.length > 0){
plv8.elog(NOTICE, "servicions");
r.service = service_request.service;
var token = '';
if(service_request.cookies && service_request.cookies.sessionIDSystem){
token = service_request.cookies;
}
plv8.elog(NOTICE, "Obtuvo Tokken");
			try{

// Revisa que la funcion exista
var fun_service = plv8.find_function('services.funjs_'+service_request.service);
// Revisa que el servicio este habilitado para ser consumido				
var service = plv8.execute( 'SELECT services.fun_check_service($1::TEXT, $2::TEXT);', [ service_request.service, token ] )[0].fun_check_service;

plv8.elog(NOTICE, "Termina de hacer la consulta fun_check_service");
switch(service.error){
	case 0:
R.push(fun_service(service_request));	
/*
	service_request.request.forEach(function(req){
		plv8.elog(NOTICE, "req = ", JSON.stringify(req));
		
	});
	*/

	break;
	default:
	r.message = service.message;
	r.error = service.error+4;
	R.push(r);
	break;
}

}catch(e){
	r.message = e.message;
	r.error = 2;
    R.push(r);
}

}else{
plv8.elog(NOTICE, "Did not specify the service");
	r.message = 'Did not specify the service';
	r.error = 1;
    R.push(r);
}


}else{
	r.message = 'Did not specify the body or cookies';
	r.error = 3;
    R.push(r);
}


return R;

Function: users.user_login(inotes text, iuser_agent text, iip inet, ipwd text, iuser text)

Returns: json

Language: PLPGSQL

DECLARE
_iduser BIGINT;
_idlogin BIGINT;
_token_agent UUID;
_token UUID;
R JSON;
BEGIN

SELECT iduser INTO _iduser FROM users.users WHERE username = iuser AND pwd = md5(ipwd) AND enabled = TRUE;

IF _iduser IS NOT NULL OR _iduser > 0  THEN
	--R := json_build_object('iduser', _iduser,'bar',2);
    _token_agent := md5(iip::TEXT||iuser_agent)::UUID;
    
-- SELECT l.idlogin, l.id, l.motive, t.token, t.token_agent FROM users.login l, users.tokens t WHERE l.idlogin = t.idlogin;    

IF EXISTS(SELECT COUNT(*) FROM users.login l, users.tokens t WHERE l.idlogin = t.idlogin AND l.id = _iduser AND motive = 0) THEN
-- Elimina el token y hace un logout de ese usuario
	DELETE FROM users.tokens WHERE users.tokens.idlogin = (SELECT l.idlogin FROM users.login l, users.tokens t WHERE l.idlogin = t.idlogin AND l.id = _iduser AND motive = 0 LIMIT 1);
-- Revisar cual mismo seria el motivo
    INSERT INTO users.user_login (id, motive, ip, user_agent, notes) VALUES (_iduser, 7, iip, iuser_agent, 'Logout by relogin');
END IF;

    INSERT INTO users.user_login (id, motive, ip, user_agent) VALUES (_iduser, 0, iip, iuser_agent) RETURNING idlogin INTO _idlogin;

IF _idlogin IS NOT NULL OR _idlogin > 0  THEN
    _token := md5(_idlogin::TEXT||iuser_agent||now()::TEXT)::UUID;
	INSERT INTO users.tokens(token, idlogin, token_agent, last_heartbeat) VALUES (_token, _idlogin, _token_agent, now());    
	R := json_build_object('return', json_build_object('iduser',_iduser,'token', _token), 'error', 0, 'message', '');
    
    --var R = {return: {iduser: 0, token: ''}, error: 0, message: ''};
ELSE
	R := json_build_object('error',2,'message','No se pudo insertar en user_login');
END IF;
    
ELSE
	R := json_build_object('error',1,'message','Invalid username or password');
END IF;

RETURN R;
END;

Function: users.user_logout(inotes uuid, iuser_agent inet, iip text, itoken text)

Returns: json

Language: PLPGSQL

DECLARE
_token_agent UUID;
_idlogin BIGINT;
_iduser BIGINT;
R JSON;
BEGIN
  _token_agent := md5(iip::TEXT||iuser_agent)::UUID;
  SELECT l.idlogin, l.id INTO _idlogin, _iduser FROM users.login l, users.tokens t WHERE l.idlogin = t.idlogin AND t.token = itoken AND token_agent = _token_agent LIMIT 1;
DELETE FROM users.tokens WHERE users.tokens.idlogin = _idlogin;
    INSERT INTO users.user_login (id, motive, ip, user_agent, notes) VALUES (_iduser, 1, iip, iuser_agent, inotes);
R := json_build_object('return', true, 'error', 0, 'message', '');
RETURN R;
END;

Function: users.user_on_insert_update()

Returns: trigger

Language: PLPGSQL

BEGIN


--  Creamos un username si no es proporcionado
IF NEW.username IS NULL OR LENGTH(NEW.username) < 1 THEN
SELECT identification INTO NEW.username FROM contacts.contacts WHERE idcontact = NEW.idcontact;
END IF;

-- creamos una clave igual al md5 del user_name si no es proporcionada.
IF NEW.pwd IS NULL OR LENGTH(NEW.pwd) < 1 THEN
 NEW.pwd := md5(NEW.username::TEXT); 
END IF;

/*
-- Clave como md5
IF TG_OP = 'UPDATE' THEN
NEW.admin_pwd := md5(NEW.admin_pwd::TEXT);
END IF;
*/

-- setea end_date = a start_date si la fecha end_date es menor que start_date
IF NEW.user_end < NEW.user_start OR NEW.user_end IS NULL THEN  
NEW.user_end := NEW.user_start + interval '5 year';
END IF;  

RETURN NEW;
END;
